 The most important job of the Central Reserve Bank of India is to communicate new and old currency in the country
 isamen nai karency or nae sikkon kaa deshbhar main vitaran, puraani karency ko risical karnaa or sabhi bainkon main ekatra hue atyadhik cash ko apane paas rakhane kaa kaam kiya jaataa he
 To do all these things, the Reserve Bank has to make many treasuries across the country, which it calls currency chests
 is karency chest yaa kuber ke khajaane ko deshbhar kai jagahon par banaaya jaataa he jisase rigerv bank kaa karency vitaran kaam aasaani se kiya ja sake
 Currently, the Reserve Bank has about 4211 currency chests to maintain currency communications across the country
 iske alaava sikkon kaa sanchaalan karne ke liye uske paas 3990 depo hai
 These chests are spread all over the country because along with the communication, these treasures also hold the deposits (cash reserve ratio) deposited in any common bank
 notebandi kii prakriya shuru hote hi ye karency chest mahatvapurn bhoomika nibhaa rahe hai
 After printing new currency in government love, it is delivered directly to these currency chests spread across the country
 rigerv bank kaa diya yah nakshaa bataata he ki desh main kahaan-kahaan karency chest maujuud hai
 The Reserve Bank takes the support of the state-run Bank of India, the leading public sector bank, to set up a partnership chest in the country
 iske alaava is kaam main 6 sahyogi bainkon, sabhi naishanalined bank, privet sector ke kuch chune hue bank, 1 videshi bank, 1 kooparative bank or gramin bank ko bhi shaamil kiya jaataa he
 The Reserve Bank does this through its 18 branches or issue offices spread across the country
 kaise pahunchaai jaati he chest main karencidesh ke 4 sarkari press main karency kii printing hone ke baad use sidhe rigerv bank ke 18 ishu offis main pahunchaaya jaataa he
 The help of railways, air force cargo carriers and state police are taken to reach the new currency to these offices
 shaharon main yatayaat ke liye aamtaur par karency kii badi movement ke liye nijee kshetra se bade container vehical kiraye par liye jate hai
 The entire confidentiality of this entire process is maintained and in some sensitive areas of the country, the help of the army is also taken for security
 iske baad karency ko rigerv bank kii nigaraanee main anya bainkon dwaara chalaae ja rahe karency chest main pahunchaa diya jaataa he
 atms and bank branches get the currency from this huge network of Reserve Bank, the currency is put in the banking system
 isamen pramukh kaam deshbhar main sabhi bainkon ke atm main rupaya bharne ke kaam ke saath-saath bank kii sabhi branchon main din ke kaam ke liye karency kii supplai kii jaati he
 US President Barack Obama, while hailing the families of victims of a shootout in a Connecticut school, has said that the country is not doing enough to keep their children safe and that they have taken their positions to prevent such 'tragedies' Promised to use the power of

 ) Skymet, a private weather forecasting company, said on Tuesday that the monsoon could hit Kerala on June 4, marking the official start of the rainy season in the country
 bataa den ki kerala main saamanyat: monsoon ke aagaman kii taarikh ek june he
 Skymet CEO Jatin Singh said that all four regions are going to receive less than normal rainfall this season
 purv or purvottar bharat tathaa madhya hisse barish ke maamle main uttar pashchim bharat or dakshini prayadweep se kharaab sthiti main rahenge
 Monsoon will start around June 4
 aisa lagata he ki bhartiya prayadweep main monsoon kaa shuruaati charan dhimaa hone ja rahaa he
 The monsoon is likely to reach Andaman and Nicobar islands on 22 May
 gat maheene skymet ne mausam ke liye saamaanya se kam monsoon rahane kaa anumaan jataayaa tha
 Significantly, Skymet, a private weather forecasting agency, said that the monsoon may receive less than normal rainfall this year
 agency ne sambhavit saamaanya se kam barish ke peeche kii vajah alanino ko bataaya he
 The agency said the monsoon is expected to be 93 per cent of its long-term average (LPA)
 darasal alpie kii 90-95 fisadi barish saamaanya se kam vaali shrenee main aati he
 The average of the total rainfall between 1951 and 2000 is called LPA and is 89 cm
 yadi yah purvanumaan sahi sabit hota he to yah lagaataar doosraa varsh hoga jab saamaanya se kam barish hogi
 There may be the highest risk of decreasing rainfall in eastern India
 purvanumaan main kaha gaya he ki odisha, chhattisgarh or tateey andhra pradesh main puure mausam main saamaanya barish hone kii sambhaavna he
 Skymet CEO Jatin Singh said that in June the LPA may get 77 percent of the rainfall, while in July the LPA may get 91 percent of the rain
 singh ne bataaya ki purvanumaan ke anusaar june or july main saamaanya se kam barish hone kii sambhaavna he
 LPA can receive 102 percent and 99 percent rainfall in August and September
 skymet ne sambhavit saamaanya se kam barish ke peeche al-nino ko jimmedaar tehraaya he
 Skymet President (meteorology and Climate Change) Air Vice Marshal (retd) GP Sharma said that el-nino has an effect on the monsoon
 unhone kaha, ‘‘prashanth mahaasaagar ausat se adhik garm ho gaya he
 El Niño has an 80 percent probability in estimates during March – May, which falls to 60 percent from June to August
